	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '55bc6cc735f224692f9e9deba36e616b8fa2899f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '55bc6cc735f224692f9e9deba36e616b8fa2899f') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '825e5c386e56356aa8c8e79626a26359f208feab') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '55bc6cc735f224692f9e9deba36e616b8fa2899f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/frdl/publicPages/1276945_rdap/manifest.xml');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('plugins/frdl/publicPages/1276945_rdap/manifest.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/frdl/publicPages/1276945_rdap/manifest.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/frdl/publicPages/1276945_rdap/manifest.xml') != 'b0a3bbc8b52fa654393b61b33a5cabdcaa36418f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/frdl/publicPages/1276945_rdap/manifest.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/frdl/publicPages/1276945_rdap/manifest.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/frdl/publicPages/1276945_rdap/manifest.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/frdl/publicPages/1276945_rdap/manifest.xml') !== 'b0a3bbc8b52fa654393b61b33a5cabdcaa36418f') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/frdl/publicPages/1276945_rdap/manifest.xml') !== 'df968d6513b4eee9177bba08cdd27fc80241326e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/frdl/publicPages/1276945_rdap/manifest.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/frdl/publicPages/1276945_rdap/manifest.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/frdl/publicPages/1276945_rdap/manifest.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/frdl/publicPages/1276945_rdap/manifest.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/frdl/publicPages/1276945_rdap/manifest.xml') !== 'b0a3bbc8b52fa654393b61b33a5cabdcaa36418f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/frdl/publicPages/1276945_rdap/manifest.xml');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.json');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.json')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') != 'cab969bf183af133e18ff72751952b5f6aa01c3d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.json', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.json');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'cab969bf183af133e18ff72751952b5f6aa01c3d') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== '1992e2178d439a52a7721ab25588434b5ef5c278') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.json');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.json')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.json', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.json') !== 'cab969bf183af133e18ff72751952b5f6aa01c3d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.json');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/composer/installed.php');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('vendor/composer/installed.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') != '995c959b856f9e74953cd551b08ff1344ef98a17') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/composer/installed.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/composer/installed.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '995c959b856f9e74953cd551b08ff1344ef98a17') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== 'e397fe11aa6c2150e1aa57a6f442453d63ca9838') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/composer/installed.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/composer/installed.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/composer/installed.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/composer/installed.php') !== '995c959b856f9e74953cd551b08ff1344ef98a17') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/composer/installed.php');
		}
	}
}
